```jsx
// Fix 1 (R2): rendered-data aggregates across ALL guests (self + others) for Â«Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð»Â» header
const renderedTableTotal = React.useMemo(() => {
  let total = 0;
  const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
  allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
    const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
    orders.forEach((o) => {
      if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled') {
        total += Number(o.total_amount) || 0;
      }
    });
  });
  return parseFloat(total.toFixed(2));
}, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);

// Fix 1 (R2): dish count = sum of item quantities (same semantics as ordersItemCount line 789-792)
const renderedTableDishCount = React.useMemo(() => {
  let count = 0;
  const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
  allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
    const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
    orders.forEach((o) => {
      if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled') return;
      const items = itemsByOrder.get(o.id) || [];
      count += items.reduce((s, it) => s + (it.quantity || 1), 0);
    });
  });
  return count;
}, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders, itemsByOrder]);

// Fix 1 (R2): guest count = self (if has orders) + others
const renderedTableGuestCount = React.useMemo(() => {
  const selfCount = myGuestId && ordersByGuestId.has(myGuestId) ? 1 : 0;
  return selfCount + otherGuestIdsFromOrders.length;
}, [myGuestId, ordersByGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);
```

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 2.1** â€” ÐžÐ±Ð½Ð¾Ð²Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ `statusBuckets` (ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐ¸ 456-467) Ð´Ð¾Ð±Ð°Ð²Ð»ÐµÐ½Ð¸ÐµÐ¼ `pending_unconfirmed` Ð³Ñ€ÑƒÐ¿Ð¿Ñ‹:

```jsx
const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
  const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [] };
  todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
    const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
    const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
      || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes((o.status || '').toLowerCase()));
    const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && (o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled';
    if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
    else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
  });
  return groups;
}, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
```

**Ð—Ð°Ð¼ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð½Ð°:**
```jsx
const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
  const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [], pending_unconfirmed: [] };
  todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
    const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
    const rawStatus = (o.status || '').toLowerCase();
    const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
      || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes(rawStatus));
    const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'cancelled';
    // Fix 2 (R1): pending_unconfirmed = 'submitted' status (awaiting waiter confirmation).
    // Priority: server-side stageInfo wins; only raw status === 'submitted' AND no stage info â†’ pending.
    const isPending = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'submitted';

    if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
    else if (isPending) groups.pending_unconfirmed.push(o);
    else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
  });
  return groups;
}, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
```

```jsx
              {/* Self orders â€” always expanded (CV-16) */}
              <div className="pl-2 border-l-2 border-slate-200 space-y-1">
                {myOrdersInSession.map((order) => {
                  const items = itemsByOrder.get(order.id) || [];
                  const status = getSafeStatus(getOrderStatus(order));
                  const isOrderPending = (order.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'submitted';

                  if (items.length === 0) {
                    return (
                      <div key={order.id} className="flex justify-between items-center text-xs">
                        <span className="text-slate-600">
                          {tr('cart.order_total', 'Ð¡ÑƒÐ¼Ð¼Ð° Ð·Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·Ð°')}: {formatPrice(parseFloat(Number(order.total_amount).toFixed(2)))}
                          {isOrderPending && (
                            <span className="ml-1 text-amber-600 font-medium">â³ {tr('cart.order.pending_badge', 'ÐžÐ¶Ð¸Ð´Ð°ÐµÑ‚')}</span>
                          )}
                        </span>
                        <span className="text-xs" style={{ color: status.color }}>{status.icon} {status.label}</span>
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  return items.map((item, idx) => (
                    <div key={`${order.id}-${idx}`} className="flex justify-between items-center text-xs">
                      <span className="text-slate-600">
                        {item.dish_name} Ã— {item.quantity}
                        {isOrderPending && (
                          <span className="ml-1 text-amber-600 font-medium">â³ {tr('cart.order.pending_badge', 'ÐžÐ¶Ð¸Ð´Ð°ÐµÑ‚')}</span>
                        )}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-xs" style={{ color: status.color }}>{status.icon} {status.label}</span>
                    </div>
                  ));
                })}
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        );
      })()}
```

   9: function lightenColor(hex, amount) {
  10:   const num = parseInt(hex.replace('#', ''), 16);
  11:   const r = Math.min(255, (num >> 16) + Math.round((255 - (num >> 16)) * amount));
  12:   const g = Math.min(255, ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF) + Math.round((255 - ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF)) * amount));
  13:   const b = Math.min(255, (num & 0x0000FF) + Math.round((255 - (num & 0x0000FF)) * amount));
  14:   return `#${(r << 16 | g << 8 | b).toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`;
  15: }

# Codex Reviewer Findings — ПССК Prompt Quality Review
Chain: pssk-cv-b2-260416-v4-260416-184426-432b

## Issues Found
1. [MEDIUM] i18n exception contradicts scope lock and misstates fallback behavior — The prompt says scope is only `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx`, then later says 11 new dictionary keys “MUST” be added elsewhere. In this file, `tr()` already falls back to the provided Russian string when a key is missing (`CartView.jsx` lines 282-287), so the claim that missing keys will render raw ids like `cart.group.pending` is incorrect. PROMPT FIX: either keep the batch scoped to `CartView.jsx` and rely on `tr(key, fallback)` here, or explicitly widen scope and name the dictionary file; remove the claim that missing keys leak raw keys in this component.
2. [MEDIUM] Fix 3 persistence implementation breaks the frozen R4 contract — R4 requires durable persist keyed per table as `cv_terminal_dismissed_{tableId}`, but Fix 3 uses one global key `cv_terminal_dismissed` holding a single table id. That loses dismissal history when the guest visits another table and can make a previously dismissed closed table show the terminal again. PROMPT FIX: read/write `cv_terminal_dismissed_${currentTableKey}` or equivalent per-table key, and update the grep and acceptance text to match that contract.
3. [MEDIUM] Fix 3 depends on unverified `currentTable.id` — The prompt correctly disproves `currentTable.status`, but it never proves that `currentTable.id` exists in this component. The live file only shows `currentTable?.name` / `currentTable?.code` usage (`CartView.jsx` line 385). If `id` is missing, `showTerminal` stays false and the new screen never appears. PROMPT FIX: add a verification step proving `currentTable.id`, or derive the durable key from a verified fallback such as `currentTable?.id ?? currentTable?.code ?? currentTable?.name`.
4. [LOW] Fix 2 under-specifies how `'submitted'` interacts with `getOrderStatus()` — The prompt only verifies raw `o.status === 'submitted'` via `submittedTableTotal` (`CartView.jsx` line 528), but its patch places an order into `pending_unconfirmed` only when `!stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'submitted'`. If `getOrderStatus(o)` already returns an internal code for submitted orders, they will remain in `in_progress`, so the UX requirement can fail. PROMPT FIX: explicitly verify how `getOrderStatus()` represents submitted orders, or make the prompt state which signal wins and update the patch accordingly.

## Summary
Total: 4 issues (0 CRITICAL, 3 MEDIUM, 1 LOW)

## Additional Risks
- Fix 2’s suggested header class interpolation uses dynamic Tailwind classes, which conflicts with the repo rule to avoid dynamic Tailwind class construction and may trigger review churn even if it renders correctly.
- The mobile/regression checklist is detailed, but the prompt does not specify a concrete harness or tool for the 375px validation, so that part may be skipped or inconsistently performed.

## Prompt Clarity (MANDATORY — do NOT skip)
- Overall clarity: 4/5
- What was most clear: Fix 1 and Fix 4 are well anchored to live source lines; the prompt correctly identifies `bucketDisplayNames`, `showTableOrdersSection`, `otherGuestIdsFromOrders`, and the current header/table render blocks.
- What was ambiguous or could cause hesitation: whether `currentTable.id` is guaranteed, whether `'submitted'` ever coexists with `stageInfo.internal_code`, and whether the task is truly single-file once the i18n exception is applied.
- Missing context: the actual i18n dictionary path, the contract for `currentTable` identity, and the expected `getOrderStatus()` output for pre-acceptance orders.
